The lady at the front desk saw that we arrived late, so she delayed our check-out and upgraded our room for free. The hotel also provided free parking and registered our license plate number for us. Our room was also on a higher floor, with a bathtub in the room and welcome fruits. Thanks to Miss Amanda from GRO for drawing the welcome card. The bathrobes in the hotel were also very comfortable, and we slept very well all night. When we checked out in the morning, the front desk also thoughtfully packed up the breakfast we didn't have for us to take away. This hotel is really worth considering for holidays, and the price/performance ratio is also very good. After all, five-star hotels in Beijing are much more expensive in comparison. Later, Amanda called me back to inquire about the accommodation. I hope to meet this thoughtful lady next time I come to stay.
